## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class SupportedLanguages {
        +String Chinese~Simplified~ : zh
        +String Dutch : nl
        +String English : en
        +String French : fr
        +String French~Canadian~ : fr-CA
        +String German : de
        +String Italian : it
        +String Polish : pl
        +String Russian : ru
        +String Spanish : es
        +String Portugese : pt
    }
    class LanguageModule {
        +findSupportedLanguage(locale) String
    }
    LanguageModule ..> SupportedLanguages : uses
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> CheckLocale
    CheckLocale --> ReturnFalse: locale is null/undefined
    CheckLocale --> ExactMatch: locale exists
    ExactMatch --> ReturnLanguage: found in SupportedLanguages
    ExactMatch --> ParseLocale: not found
    ParseLocale --> BaseLanguageMatch: split by hyphen
    BaseLanguageMatch --> ReturnLanguage: base language found
    BaseLanguageMatch --> ReturnFallback: not found
    ReturnFalse --> [*]
    ReturnLanguage --> [*]
    ReturnFallback --> [*]
```
